  jmp    launch\nchk     jmz.b  setscan, res\n        jmp    launch\nsetscan mov.b  #1, mode\n        stp.b  mode, _MODE\nlaunch  jmz.b  flash_start, mode\n        jmp    comp\nmode    dat    #0,
